Based on the 2024 CCAR results, the Corporation&#8217;s stress capital buffer (&#8220;SCB&#8221;) will be 3.2% and the CET1 minimum requirement will be 10.7% when finalized. This new SCB will be effective from October 1, 2024 to September 30, 2025. At March 31, 2024, the Corporation had $197 billion of regulatory CET1 capital and a CET1 ratio of 11.9% which exceeds its current regulatory minimum requirement of 10.0%.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">A
